\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__samples__generator_8py_source_l01984}01984\ \ \ \ \ t\ =\ 3\ *\ np.pi\ *\ (generator.uniform(size=(1,\ n\_samples))\ -\/\ 0.5)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__samples__generator_8py_source_l01985}01985\ \ \ \ \ X\ =\ np.empty(shape=(n\_samples,\ 3),\ dtype=np.float64)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__samples__generator_8py_source_l01986}01986\ \ \ \ \ X[:,\ 0]\ =\ np.sin(t)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__samples__generator_8py_source_l01987}01987\ \ \ \ \ X[:,\ 1]\ =\ 2.0\ *\ generator.uniform(size=n\_samples)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__samples__generator_8py_source_l01988}01988\ \ \ \ \ X[:,\ 2]\ =\ np.sign(t)\ *\ (np.cos(t)\ -\/\ 1)}
